<h1 class="post-title">
<span class="the-title">(New Normal) Winter is Coming</span> </h1>
<div class="post-author">
<a href="https://off-guardian.org/author/admin/" title="All posts by Editor">Editor</a> </div>
</div>
<div class="post_page-content post">
<h6>CJ Hopkins</h6>
<a href="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/new-normal-winter.jpg?x46269"><img alt="" class="aligncenter size-offg-header-image wp-image-78998" decoding="async" height="900" src="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/new-normal-winter-1920x900.jpg?x46269" width="1920"/></a>
<h3 style="font-size: 150%; margin-bottom: 0;">Audio Version <span style="color: RGB(150,0,50)"><sup>New Feature!</sup></span></h3>
<div class="audio-container" style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
<!--[if lt IE 9]><script>document.createElement('audio');</script><![endif]-->
<audio class="wp-audio-shortcode" controls="controls" id="audio-78991-1" preload="none" style="width: 100%;"><source src="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/New-Normal-Winter-is-Coming-Edit-1-MONO.mp3?_=1" type="audio/mpeg"/><a href="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/New-Normal-Winter-is-Coming-Edit-1-MONO.mp3">https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/New-Normal-Winter-is-Coming-Edit-1-MONO.mp3</a></audio>
</div>
<p class="dropcap">Winter is coming…and you know what that means. That’s right, it’s nearly time once again for the global-capitalist ruling classes to whip the New Normal masses into a state of mindless mass hysteria over an imaginary apocalyptic virus.</p>
<p>The same imaginary apocalyptic virus that they have whipped the New Normal masses into a state of mass hysteria over throughout the Winter for the last two years.</p>
<p>They’ve got their work cut out for them this time. Seriously, how much more mass hysterical could the New Normals possibly get at this point?</p>
<p>The vast majority of the Western world has been transformed into a pseudo-medical dystopia in which you have to show your “health-purity papers” to enter a café and get a cup of coffee.</p>
<p>People who refuse to get experimentally “vaccinated” against <a href="https://swprs.org/studies-on-covid-19-lethality/#hospitalizations">a virus that causes mild-to-moderate symptoms (or, often, no symptoms whatsoever) in about 95% of the infected</a>, and <a href="https://swprs.org/studies-on-covid-19-lethality/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">the overall infection fatality rate of which is approximately </a><a href="https://swprs.org/studies-on-covid-19-lethality/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">0.1% to 0.5%</a>, are being systematically segregated, stripped of their jobs, denied medical treatment, demonized as “a danger to society,” censored, fined, and otherwise persecuted.</p>
<p>If you think I’m overstating the case, look at the front page of this Australian newspaper…</p>
<a href="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming.jpg?x46269"><img alt="" class="unfiltered aligncenter size-offg-body-image-650 wp-image-78997" decoding="async" height="773" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" src="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming-650x773.jpg?x46269" srcset="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming-650x773.jpg 650w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming-500x594.jpg 500w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming-768x913.jpg 768w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming-800x951.jpg 800w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/australia-headline-most-wanted-cj-winter-is-coming.jpg 842w" width="650"/></a>
<p>Yes, <a href="https://consentfactory.org/2021/10/12/the-great-new-normal-purge/">the Great New Normal Purge</a> is on. “The Unvaccinated” and other infidels and heretics are being hunted by fanatical, hate-drunk mobs, dragged before the New Normal Inquisition, and made examples of all over the world.</p>
<p>Here in New Normal Germany, popular footballer <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-59048800">Joshua Kimmich is being publicly drawn and quartered</a> for refusing to submit to being “vaccinated” and profess his faith in the New Normal World Order. </p>
<p>In the USA, <a href="https://slate.com/news-and-politics/2021/10/colin-powell-vaccinated-covid-anti-vaxxers-endanger-others.html">“the Unvaccinated” stand accused of murdering Colin Powell</a>, an 84-year-old, cancer-ridden war criminal. </p>
<p>Australia is planning to <a href="https://www.theage.com.au/politics/victoria/two-year-jail-terms-loom-for-health-order-breaches-under-pandemic-laws-20211026-p59349.html">imprison people and fine them $90,000</a> for the “crime” of not wearing a medical-looking mask, or <a href="https://twitter.com/consent_factory/status/1435189761598177280">attempted worship at a synagogue</a>, or whatever. </p>
<p>In Florida (of all places), <a href="https://twitter.com/consent_factory/status/1452339723536584704">fanatical school staff tied a medical-looking mask to the face of a non-verbal Downs-syndrome girl with nylon cord</a>, day after day, for over six weeks, until her father discovered what they were doing.</p>
<p>I could go on, but I don’t think I have to. The Internet is brimming with examples of mass-hysterical and sadistic behavior.</p>
<p>And that’s not to mention the mass hysteria rampant among the New Normals themselves…for example, the parents who are lining up to get their children needlessly “vaccinated” and then rushed into the emergency room with “totally manageable myocarditis.”</p>
<a href="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax.jpg?x46269"><img alt="" class="aligncenter size-offg-body-image-650 wp-image-78993" decoding="async" height="773" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px" src="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax-650x773.jpg?x46269" srcset="https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax-650x773.jpg 650w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax-500x595.jpg 500w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax-768x914.jpg 768w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax-800x952.jpg 800w, https://off-guardian.org/wp-content/medialibrary/shane-huntington-creepy-tweet-ill-son-pfizer-vax.jpg 811w" width="650"/></a>
<p>Still, as mass hysterical as things are, count on GloboCap to go balls out on the mass hysteria for the next five months. The coming Winter is crunch time, folks. They need to cement the New Normal in place, so they can dial down the “apocalyptic pandemic.” If they’re forced to extend it another year…well, not even the most brainwashed New Normals would buy that.</p>
<p>Or…all right, sure, the <em>most </em>brainwashed would, but they represent a small minority. Most New Normals are not fanatical totalitarians. They’re just people looking out for themselves, people who will go along with almost anything to avoid being ostracized and punished.</p>
<p>But, believe it or not, there <em>is </em>a limit to the level of absurdity they’re prepared to accept, and the level and duration of relentless stress and cognitive dissonance they are prepared to accept.</p>
<p>Most of them have reached that limit. They have done their part, followed orders, worn the masks, got the “vaccinations,” and are happy to present their “obedience papers” to anyone who demands to see them. Now, they want to go back to “normal.” But they can’t, because … well, because of us.</p>
<p>See, GloboCap can’t let them return to “normal” (i.e., the new totalitarian version of “normal”) until everyone (i.e., everyone who matters) has submitted to being “vaccinated” and is walking around with a scanable certificate of ideological conformity in their smartphones.</p>
<p>They would probably even waive the “vaccination” requirement if we would just bend the knee and pledge our allegiance to the WEF, or BlackRock, or Vanguard, or whoever, and carry around a QR code confirming that we believe in “Science,” the “Covidian Creed,” and whatever other ecumenical corporatist dogma.</p>
<p>Seriously, the point of this entire exercise (or at least this phase of this entire exercise) is to radically, irrevocably, transform society into a monolithic corporate campus where everyone has to scan their IDs at every turn of an endless maze of perpetually monitored, eco-friendly, gender-fluid, ideologically uniform, non-smoking, totally meat-free “safe spaces” owned and operated by GloboCap, or one of its agents, subsidiaries, and assigns.</p>
<p>The global-capitalist ruling classes are determined to transform the planet into this fascistic Woke Utopia and enforce unwavering conformity to its valueless values, no matter the cost, and we, “the Unvaccinated,” are standing in their way.</p>
<p>They can’t just round us up and shoot us — this is global capitalism, not Nazism or Stalinism. They need to break us, to break our spirits, to coerce, gaslight, harass, and persecute us until we surrender our autonomy willingly. And they need to do this during the next five months.</p>
<p>Preparations therefor are now in progress.</p>
<p>In the UK, <a href="https://www.reuters.com/world/uk/britains-covid-19-cases-down-nearly-10-over-past-week-2021-10-28/">despite a drop in “cases,”</a> and the fact (which the “authorities” have been forced to acknowledge) that <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/health-59077036">the “Vaccinated” can spread the virus just like “the Unvaccinated,”</a> <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2021/oct/23/uk-government-paves-way-to-bring-in-tough-plan-b-covid-rules">the government is preparing to go to “Plan B”</a> and roll out the social-segregation system that most of Europe has already adopted.</p>
<p>In Germany, the “Epidemic Emergency of National Importance” (i.e., the legal pretense for enforcement of the “Corona restrictions”) is due to expire in mid-November (unless they can seriously jack up the “cases,” which seems unlikely at this point), so <a href="https://www.dw.com/en/covid-germany-set-to-end-national-state-of-emergency/a-59637132">the authorities are working to revise the “Infektionsschutzgesetz” (the “Infection Protection Act”) to justify maintaining the restrictions indefinitely, despite the absence of an “epidemic,” or an “emergency.”</a></p>
<p>And so on. I think you get the picture. </p>
<p>This Winter is probably going to get a little nutty … or, OK, more than a little nutty. In terms of manufactured mass hysteria, it is probably going to make Russiagate, the <a href="https://www.nakedcapitalism.com/2020/11/the-liberals-new-passion-for-snobbery-and-censorship-an-interview-review-of-the-war-on-populism-and-trumpocalypse-by-c-j-hopkins.html">War on Populism</a>, the Global War on Terror, the Red Scare, and every other manufactured mass-hysteria campaign you can possibly think of look like an amateur production of Wagner’s <em>Götterdammerung</em>.</p>
<p>In other words, kiss reality (or whatever is left of reality at this point) goodbye. The clock is ticking, and GloboCap knows it. If they expect to pull this <a href="https://winteroak.org.uk/the-great-reset/">Great Reset</a> off, they are going to need to terrorize the New-Normal masses into a state of protracted pants-shitting panic and uncontrollable mindless hatred of “the Unvaccinated,” and anyone challenging their rule.</p>
<p>A repeat of the Winters of 2020 and 2021 is not going to cut it. It is going to take more than the now standard repertoire of fake and manipulated statistics, dire projections, photos of “death trucks,” non-overflowing overflowing hospitals, and all the other familiar features of the neo-Goebbelsian propaganda juggernaut we have been subjected to for over 18 months.</p>
<p>They are facing <a href="https://www.tabletmag.com/sections/news/articles/revolt-essential-workers">a growing working-class revolt</a>. Millions of people in countries all over the world are protesting in the streets, organizing strikes, walk-outs, “sick-outs,” and mounting other forms of opposition. </p>
<p>Despite the corporate media’s Orwellian attempts to blackout any coverage of it, or demonize us all as “far-right extremists,” the New Normals are very aware that this is happening. And the official narrative is finally falling apart. <a href="https://off-guardian.org/2021/09/22/30-facts-you-need-to-know-your-covid-cribsheet/">The actual facts are undeniable by anyone with an ounce of integrity</a>, so much so that <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2021/oct/28/covid-vaccinated-likely-unjabbed-infect-cohabiters-study-suggests">even major GloboCap propaganda outlets like <em>The Guardian</em> are being forced to grudgingly admit the truth</a>.</p>
<p>No, GloboCap has no choice at this point but to let loose with every weapon in its arsenal — <a href="https://consentfactory.org/2021/09/02/the-covidian-cult-part-iii/">short of full-blown despotism, which it cannot deploy without destroying itself</a> — and hope that we will finally break down, bend the knee, and beg for mercy.</p>
<p>I don’t know exactly what they’ve got in mind, but I am definitely not looking forward to it. I’m already pretty worn out as it is. From what I gather, so are a lot of you. If it helps at all, maybe look at it this way. We don’t have to take the battle to them. All we have to do is not surrender, withstand the coming siege, and make it to April.</p>
<p>Or, if the <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-58913865">strikes</a>, <a href="https://nypost.com/2021/10/30/fdny-firehouses-shuttered-over-vaccine-staffing-shortages/?utm_campaign=iphone_nyp&amp;utm_source=message_app">sick-outs,</a> and <a href="https://edition.cnn.com/2021/10/31/business/american-airlines-cancels-flights-sunday/index.html?utm_source=twcnnbrk&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_term=link&amp;utm_content=2021-10-31T13%3A03%3A33">“bad weather”</a> continue, it might not even take that long.</p>
<h6 class="author">CJ Hopkins is an award-winning American playwright, novelist and political satirist based in Berlin. His plays are published by Bloomsbury Publishing and Broadway Play Publishing, Inc. His dystopian novel, <a href="https://www.amazon.com/exec/obidos/ASIN/3000555269/counterpunchmaga" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Zone 23</a>, is published by Snoggsworthy, Swaine &amp; Cormorant. Volumes I and II of his <a href="https://www.amazon.com/C-J-Hopkins/e/B00CH7L382/ref=dp_byline_cont_pop_book_1">Consent Factory Essays</a> are published by Consent Factory Publishing, a wholly-owned subsidiary of Amalgamated Content, Inc. He can be reached at <a href="https://cjhopkins.com/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">cjhopkins.com</a> or <a href="https://consentfactory.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">consentfactory.org</a>.</h6>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>David Jenkins – cause of death still not disclosed</p>
<p><a href="https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-10083055/Diving-coach-worked-Tom-Daley-Team-GB-Tokyo-Olympics-dies-aged-31.html" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-10083055/Diving-coach-worked-Tom-Daley-Team-GB-Tokyo-Olympics-dies-aged-31.html</a><br/>
Oct 12, 2021<br/>
Tributes have poured in for Olympic diving coach David Jenkins who died ‘unexplainedly’ over the weekend aged just 31. The highly-respected coach, who had worked with diving star Tom Daley, was part of Team GB’s Tokyo 2020 training squad – which helped secure a joint-record medals haul at this year’s Olympic games. David’s death was confirmed by British Swimming and Swim England on Monday, although the cause remains unknown.  </p>
<p><a href="https://www.britishswimming.org/news/diving-news/british-swimming-express-sadness-death-david-jenkins" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.britishswimming.org/news/diving-news/british-swimming-express-sadness-death-david-jenkins</a></p>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Shockwaves felt through South Burnett following sudden death of ‘much loved’ Cherbourg elder Uncle Bevan Costello<br/>
ABC Wide Bay<br/>
Sep 16, 2021<br/>
Cherbourg elder Uncle Bevan Costello is being remembered as proud Wakka Wakka man and a passionate advocate for his community, following his sudden death. Uncle Bevan is believed to have suffered a heart attack on Wednesday morning, sending shockwaves through the community and beyond. The Cherbourg Aboriginal Shire Council described him as a much loved, respected elder, mentor and champion.<br/>
<a href="https://www.abc.net.au/news/2021-09-16/vale-uncle-bevan-costello/100466064" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.abc.net.au/news/2021-09-16/vale-uncle-bevan-costello/100466064</a><br/>
—</p>
<p>Queensland’s Indigenous communities push back against vaccine hesitancy<br/>
Sep 10, 2021<br/>
ABC News (Australia)<br/>
Aboriginal elders and teenagers are leading the push to get more people in Queensland’s Indigenous communities vaccinated. Cherbourg elder Uncle Bevan Costello this week received his second dose of the Pfizer vaccine.</p>
<p>“I feel more confident now that I’m fully vaccinated that if I come into contact with COVID I should be OK because I’m a diabetic,” Uncle Bevan said.</p>
<p>Figures released earlier this week showed only 4.6 per cent of the Cherbourg population aged over 15 were fully vaccinated. It’s among the lowest vaccination rates in the nation.</p>
<p><span class="embed-youtube" style="text-align:center; display: block;"><iframe allowfullscreen="true" class="youtube-player" height="360" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-presentation" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/o7lxhdEYh1E?version=3&amp;rel=1&amp;showsearch=0&amp;showinfo=1&amp;iv_load_policy=1&amp;fs=1&amp;hl=en-US&amp;autohide=2&amp;wmode=transparent" style="border:0;" width="640"></iframe></span></p>
</div>
<div class="wpd-comment-footer">
<div class="wpd-vote">
<div class="wpd-vote-up wpd_not_clicked">

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Leighton Costello said: “Dad had a history of chronic illness . . . Leading up to his death he was ill for a few weeks and passed away from … a heart attack. . . . My father did not pass away from the vaccination. Dad … wanted everyone to get vaccinated.”</p>
<p>My understanding is that the clinical trials to establish safety were on people who were in good health. If so, it would be negligent to give the jab to somebody who was in a state of ill health. And if the health authorities are being negligent, why would anybody trust them?</p>
</div>

Nov 3, 2021<br/>
New Zealand gang leaders unite to push vaccination uptake in hard-to-reach communities </p>
<p>Notorious members from rival street gangs have come together for a Covid-19 vaccination campaign urging New Zealand residents to get the jab. Minister for Māori Development Willie Jackson commissioned the four-minute video in an effort to encourage Covid-19 vaccination in hard-to-reach communities. The video features some of New Zealand’s most notorious gang figures from the Head Hunters, Mongrel Mob, the King Cobras and Black Power.</p>

<p>The truth is nearly 2 million Australians have already become ill from the jabs, 21% of them had to miss work and they are ignored.</p>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>The NY Times, or some or other birdcage-liner of record, yesterday posted a headsup that because lockdowns were just too effective in reducing transmission of viruses, ergo these beginning weeks of flu season may be the most intense ever, since every flu was in a sense in hiding, of sorts, and now ready to inundate a virus-weary world.</p>
<p>So……</p>
<p>I told people for months that there would be another siege of our habits this November, and just bracing for it. They killed our season in Spring of 2020, and this one lasts about 6 months, in close contact with the public, so I expect it to go the way of the dodo, or all flesh. It’s done before it started, stick a fork in it like the coming Thanksgiving Turkeys.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>And in the UK they are talking up a “super cold” or a monster cold season. So for those following along the story goes like this:</p>
<ol>
<li>Early 2020…a deadly flu virus is coming to get you</li>
<li>The actual flu vanished from the record</li>
<li>Covid caused every illness known to man</li>
<li>Then it kind of went away for the summer but…</li>
<li>Winter is coming, you need to be scared</li>
<li>But we aren’t exactly going to blame covid and its many lethal variant cousins </li>
<li>Because that would mean the injections are basically pointless</li>
<li>So we’ll keep covid kind of simmering in the background</li>
<li>While we blame the sicknesses that we will terrorise you all with</li>
<li>On a monster cold…</li>
<li>The mother of all colds…</li>
<li>Should we stay home and isolate and wear a mask when we have the common cold?</li>
<li>Of course we should because it’s for the greater good…</li>
<li> You don’t want to kill grandma do you? </li>
</ol>
<p>And we’re back to where we started from.</p>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>It’s been 10 days since the death of the first child and the authorities still haven’t discovered the cause!<br/>
—</p>
<p>Two pupils at a Newcastle-under-Lyme school die during half-term<br/>
Published: 5 hours ago<br/>
Two boys who attended the same school have died within a week of each other over the half-term break. . . . Head teacher Garrett Murray said the cause of the pupils’ deaths had not yet been established. Writing to parents, he said Mohammed, who was in year 10, died on 24 October and Harry, in year 11, six days later.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-stoke-staffordshire-59154365" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-stoke-staffordshire-59154365</a></p>
<p>Hugo Talks<br/>
2 Kids Die From Same School Within A Week<br/>
<a href="https://hugotalks.com/2021/11/03/2-kids-die-from-same-school-within-a-week-hugo-talks-lockdown" rel="nofollow ugc">https://hugotalks.com/2021/11/03/2-kids-die-from-same-school-within-a-week-hugo-talks-lockdown</a></p>

<span wpd-tooltip="Comment Link" wpd-tooltip-position="left"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-link" data-wpd-clipboard="https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/#comment-447835"></i></span>

<i class="far fa-comments"></i>
Reply to 
<a href="#comment-447714">
Lost in a dark wood
</a>
</div>
<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>I note the familiar sanctimonious emotional blackmail: we are to show respect by not speculating irresponsibly on social media etc. This recalls the immense non-sequitur after 9/11 when one angry defender of the official account objected to the “truthers” by saying, “Don’t you know nearly three thousand people died that day?”</p>
<p>But what could be more respectful to the dead that to enquire into how they died? And what could be more disrespectful than to politely just pass it over in silence?</p>
<p>Also, I note that, just as some deaths are “hushed up” from the start, there are others loudly trumpeted but which then suspiciously vanish e.g. four year old Kali Cook from Galveston County who died “of covid”, this being blasted over all the media organs – the WSW particularly relishing it. But then there was a little headline suggesting we don’t jump to conclusions till the autopsy. After which – nothing! A recent WSW piece on the deaths of young from covid forgot all about Kali.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Hashtag trending on German Twitter yesterday: #EsKoennteDeinKindSein (“It could be your child”). Case after case after case of children and young athletes suffering serious “side-effects” of the jab, including myocarditis and even sudden death.</p>
<p>Of course the Jabberers were out in force, sanctimoniously claiming that these poor kids were being “exploited” and “misused”, not by the politicians and pharma firms, and not by the media that ignore or explain-away their injuries, but <em>by the hashtag.</em></p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Sen. Johnson Holds Expert Panel On Federal Vaccine Mandates and Vaccine Injuries<br/>
Oct 28, 2021<br/>
<a href="https://www.ronjohnson.senate.gov/2021/10/media-advisory-sen-johnson-holds-expert-panel-on-federal-vaccine-mandates-and-vaccine-injuries" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.ronjohnson.senate.gov/2021/10/media-advisory-sen-johnson-holds-expert-panel-on-federal-vaccine-mandates-and-vaccine-injuries</a></p>
<p>WHAT: Panel discussion on vaccine mandates and the consequences and the lack of compassion and response from federal health agencies to those who have experienced adverse events from the COVID-19 vaccine<br/>
WHEN: Tuesday, Nov. 2<br/>
WHERE: Russell Senate Office Building, Kennedy Caucus Room 325<br/>
WHO: Senator Ron Johnson (R-Wis.)</p>
<p>WASHINGTON — U.S. Sen. Ron Johnson (R-Wis.) will hold a panel discussion with doctors and medical researchers who have treated COVID-19 vaccine injuries and are researching the safety and efficacy of COVID-19 vaccines, patients who have experienced adverse events due to the COVID-19 vaccine, and vaccine mandates. The senator will speak to his advocacy for early treatment, the importance of American’s health care freedom and recognizing natural immunity, the impacts of mandates on the American workforce and the economy, and the lack of transparency from federal health agencies in response to his COVID-19 oversight requests.<br/>
—</p>
<p>Dr. Theresa Long; army aerospace medicine specialist.<br/>
<a href="https://brandnewtube.com/watch/theresa-long-u-s-senator-ron-johnson-holds-panel-in-dc-on-covid-19-vaccine-mandates-and-injuries_hc4tWoe2ElA9PFw.html" rel="nofollow ugc">https://brandnewtube.com/watch/theresa-long-u-s-senator-ron-johnson-holds-panel-in-dc-on-covid-19-vaccine-mandates-and-injuries_hc4tWoe2ElA9PFw.html</a></p>

<span wpd-tooltip="Comment Link" wpd-tooltip-position="left"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-link" data-wpd-clipboard="https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/#comment-447626"></i></span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Against my better judgement I checked out the Guardian article. Which does indeed report that, as we all know, and as nobody has ever denied, the ‘vaccines’ do little or nothing to reduce transmission. But this is the the conclusion we’re supposed to draw:<br/>
<em>Prof Rowland Kao, an epidemiologist at the University of Edinburgh, who was not involved in the work, said the estimates of high rates of transmission among household contacts underscored the need to vaccinate teenagers and give boosters to vulnerable people.</em><br/>
<em>“The vaccinations of younger persons to slow down transmission in the community, and the boosters to directly protect against severe infection and hospitalisation,” he said.</em><br/>
Blatant non-sequiturs like this are designed to mess with our heads and short-circuit rational thought. A classic mind control trick.</p>
</div>

<a class="wc_tw" href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=How many complete strangers does a Tesco or Aldi employe... &amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Foff-guardian.org%2F2021%2F11%2F02%2Fnew-normal-winter-is-coming%2F%23comment-447599" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" title="Share On Twitter"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fab fa-twitter wpf-cta"></i></a><a class="wc_vk" href="https://vk.com/share.php?url=https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" title="Share On VKontakte"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fab fa-vk wpf-cta"></i></a><a class="wc_ok" href="https://connect.ok.ru/offer?url=https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" title="Share On Odnoklassniki"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fab fa-odnoklassniki wpf-cta"></i></a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wpd-space"></div>
<div class="wpd-comment-link wpd-hidden">
<span wpd-tooltip="Comment Link" wpd-tooltip-position="left"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-link" data-wpd-clipboard="https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/#comment-447599"></i></span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>How many complete strangers does a Tesco or Aldi employee share the air with during an average working day? Hundreds? Thousands?</p>
<p>A full 18 months ago, “Covid” was exposed as a grotesque scam by the plainly-observable fact that supermarket workers were not dropping like flies (or dropping at all), despite spending hours every day trapped indoors among countless other air-breathing humans.</p>
<p>The eventual introduction of those ridiculous plexiglass “barriers” — apparently impassable by the wily killer-virus — was such a ballsachingly blatant attempt to prevent people from noticing the obvious.</p>
</div>

</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>A “vaccine” that does not prevent illness or transmission was never really the point. The point is the compliance to an edict and the passports which will usher in a digital currency via that QR code. While the coercion is obviously undeniable, the fact that it’s being done is the tell. Why would we all so desperately need something that doesn’t even prevent illness if not for the passports, track and trace, and complete control a digital currency will usher in for the PTB? </p>
<p>Those vaccines are not needed by ANYONE, period. The push for those who are unhealthy to have it is another tell to me. The very idea one would trust pharma to protect one if one is health compromised I will never understand. In what world has pharma ever given one shit about protecting anyone? While the point of that shot may be to kill, I tend to think our pharma masters are slathering at the idea of a continuous long revenue stream from all the injuries that don’t outright kill – think of the profit in that, think of the asset stripping that can be accomplished when one is desperate enough to survive at whatever the cost? And when one still believes, despite all evidence, that the medical establishment truly wants to “save lives.” That shot is the gift that will keep on giving, it is most certainly nothing to look forward to even without the blatant coercion.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>In the New Normal members of the medical profession can say that they are work under the ethos of the Hippocratic Oath (First do no harm) whilst also in many cases proffering the view that vaccines are safe.</p>
<p>And yet, the Merriam-Webster definition of safe is:</p>
<p>1.<strong> N</strong>ot able or likely to be hurt or harmed in any way<br/>
2. <strong>N</strong>ot able or likely to be lost, taken away<br/>
3. <strong>N</strong>ot involving or likely to involve danger, harm, or loss</p>
<p>Maybe such people should try and have a word with MW and seek a redefinition of the word ‘Safe’ or stop using it? </p>
<p>I wouldn’t be surprised if ‘Anti-Vaxxers’,’Vaccines’,’Herd Immunity’ are about to get some redefinitions in the form of some love from the Pharma/4IR/WHO gods.</p>
</div>

Reply to 
<a href="#comment-447556">
Patrick L.
</a>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Besides the global rejection of the contrived covid crisis, the smell of blood in the water over COP26 is attracting the attention of the media sharks.</p>
<p>COP 26 failed when Xi announced he wasn’t attending, then Putin, then Modi of India walked in with a demand for $1tn or he’s not playing ball. This followed 22 smaller nations presenting Kerry with a bill for $750bn in unpaid money, promised over decades of COP promises, last month. To top it off 55 other countries are demanding money with menaces to abandon any further pretence of saving the planet by stifling their countries growth at the alter of the climate crisis.</p>
<p>Boris will travel to Westminster to face the Tory big guns of David Davis, Steve Baker and Ian Duncan Smith who have already published media articles criticising his NetZero policy. That will have grown into a veritable gang during his one hour flight from Glasgow.</p>
<p>The low hanging fruit was harvested on day one with announcements of halting and reversing deforestation, promises that have been made in the past and never fulfilled. </p>
<p>There will be no meaningful decisions made, no significant agreements signed, no consensus on how to halt climate change, how can there be, the leader of the biggest emitter of CO2 boycotted the event.</p>
<p>Biden’s £3.5Tn New Green Deal is already in trouble in Congress, and now Republicans are doing well in the US in local elections. If Biden doesn’t change course uber quick on that and covid, when the 2022 midterms come round, he’ll wonder where all his support went, if he even notices.</p>
<p>Were there ever a covid crisis or a climate crisis, you can be sure this is it. The tipping point has been reached and political heads may well roll unless there is some enthusiastic back-pedalling. And you can bet we won’t be seeing much of XR and IB on the streets of the UK for much longer, they will only serve as an embarrassment to Boris.</p>
<p>It is, the perfect storm.</p>
</div>

<p>I am embarrassed to see my home town playing host to this ludicrous ruling-class jamboree. There was a time when Glaswegians were famously sceptical and miitant, a time when they had a respect for independent thought and a robust sense of the ridiculous, a time when they would have come out in force to protest against these massed gobshites. </p>

<p>Rock and roll is the sound of alcoholic machismo. Sid Vicious was the real spirit behind the Sex Pistols, and they were <strong>punk </strong>, not fucking rock’n’roll. </p>
<p>Which rock star would have the fuck-you atittude to be photographed with a nazi swastika t-shirt??</p>
<p>I suppose there is a time and place for everything. I like blasting Motorhead when the air needs clearing.</p>

<span wpd-tooltip="Comment Link" wpd-tooltip-position="left"><i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-link" data-wpd-clipboard="https://off-guardian.org/2021/11/02/new-normal-winter-is-coming/#comment-447516"></i></span>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>There’s something going on; but it’s not what any of us think. </p>
<p>For a while I thought it was the constant stress of having their lives upended; but it’s not that.</p>
<p>Something is making people inexplicably belligerent; but it’s not the machinations of the fools who believe themselves masters of the universe. </p>
<p>Something even beyond the combined effect of atmospheric spraying and electromagnetic fields like 5G.</p>
<p>Nor do I think it’s something cosmic, like astrological. Astrology doesn’t cause things; it only describes them. </p>
<p>All I can think of is some internal mechanism in our species which “knows” when the end of something is near – not because we read about it or even sensed it; but because our “genes” are alerting us to it.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>The stars show a square between transiting Uranus and Pluto in Leo, with which a whole generation, borne from the 40ies to the 60ies, is blessed. Uranus stands for radical change and Pluto for the dark, the mysterious, the inexpressable. The cycle will end in the beginning of April 22. Astrologically, it depicts deep upheavel. Whatever this means we will see.<br/>
It may well be, that the increasing belligerence is a result of fear and cognitive dissonance. And cognitive dissonance increases fear as well.</p>
<p>I believe, many have felt a change coming for a long time, before anything actually happened. Whether it applies to all of humanity, i.e. an inner knowing that a cycle is ending, is an interesting question.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>The whole Covid crisis kicking off under the conjunctions of Saturn, then Jupiter and Mars with Pluto in Capricorn in January-March 2020, is either a huge vindication of astrology OR proof that the people behind it are using astrology to time their interventions. The former I hope! Saturn/Pluto is a 38 year cycle: last conjunction 1982/3 (AIDS, rise of neoliberalism and fear of nuclear war among other things), and the opposition in late 2001 (say no more). Jupiter/Pluto describes power grabs and plutocracy, Jupiter/Saturn economic and political cycles.<br/>
Currently we’re experiencing the third square between Saturn in Aquarius and Uranus in Taurus which is all about control vs freedom.<br/>
Curious to see what will happen in the next few days with the new moon in Scorpio exactly opposite Uranus. Things are likely to get very weird, as if they weren’t already.</p>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Clearly a production – you can tell by the sound that it is staged, they are wearing voice mics, and the sound has been mixed, the interjections are too clean, the background plane noise is a perfect level, plus there is clearly additional lighting – also there are no other passengers other than the few extras you can see near the camera, even the stewardess and flight crew voices are acted…why would anyone make a video like this? To make a point I guess. Weird times we’re living through for certain</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>London seems almost normal, sure the posters and the politicians and the BBC keep pumping out the message, but most people are just carrying on, busy streets, busy shops, probably 80 percent freefacing – riding the train to the south coast, a guy behind me was coughing all over the place and sniffing loudly the entire one and a half hour journey – I happily ate my oatcakes and apple, the guy from India in the seat next to him just carried on as well, all of us maskless, made me smile</p>

<p><strong>Spain is reimbursing residents who were fined for violating COVID-19 lockdown rules</strong><br/>
<span>Around 1.1 million fines were issued to thousands of people who violated stay-at-home orders that began in the spring of 2020, reports </span><em>Insider…</em></p>
<p><a href="https://www.insider.com/spain-reimburse-those-fined-for-violating-covid-19-lockdown-rules-2021-10" rel="nofollow ugc">https://www.insider.com/spain-reimburse-those-fined-for-violating-covid-19-lockdown-rules-2021-10</a></p>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Not true. Ongoing propaganda, mask mandates indoors, quarantines for those with a cold or no symptoms, demonization of the unvaxxed. I still get calls and texts from health service zombies to get vaxxed.<br/>
Here in Spain they play a slightly different game, couldn’t say why. Most people are extremely gullible and worried about what others think of them, so there wasn’t really much need to push the New Normies too hard. The “failed” and “erroneous” governmental response to “Corona crisis” is tuning the public opinion for the totalitarian shift to come, probably by 2023.<br/>
I didn’t hear about the fines being repayed, but be clear about the fact that the stay at home orders were deemed Inconstitutional, only because of a technicism, not because they where a flagrant violation of fundamental rights under a fraudulent premise.</p>
</div>

<div class="wpd-comment-text">
<p>Wrong wrong wrong. There is no “virus”. Stop believing in “sars-cov-2” and in “viruses” and the church of virology.<br/>
They would never waive the “vaccine” requirement, because it’s a critical part of the total/centralized control, the depopulation agenda, and the transhumanist agenda.<br/>
They do not need a continued “pandemic” “emergency” – they can have other “emergencies” or even just the theoretical possibility of them (plus combinations of these).<br/>
This is not an exercise. It’s a full-on transformation attempt.<br/>
There isn’t any “Cap” anywhere, and therefore no “GloboCap”.<br/>
They can make “cases” as they like, because it is all rigged/fake.<br/>
And they can/will cause more real deaths with all the “measures”, the restrictions and destruction that comes from them, and with the injections of course.<br/>
They can use “full-blown despotism” also, as well as start another (conventional) war. They can throw everything at people everywhere.<br/>
And we most absolutely need to “take the battle to them”. If we just sit there and try to withstand, they will wipe us all out.<br/>
We need to take the battle to them, and expose their lies and show the truth and keep supporting people and helping them wake up.</p>
